Result merger: combines shard results into a single response.\\n\\nuse crate::Result;\\nuse serde_json::Value;\\nuse std::collections::{BTreeMap, BinaryHeap};\\nuse std::cmp::Ordering;\\n\\n/// A single page of hits from a shard.\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\\npub struct ShardHitPage {\\n    /// Raw JSON response from the shard.\\n    pub body: Value,\\n\\n    /// Whether this shard succeeded.\\n    pub success: bool,\\n}\\n\\n/// Input to the merge function.\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\\npub struct MergeInput {\\n    /// One page per node in the covering set.\\n    pub shard_hits: Vec<ShardHitPage>,\\n\\n    /// Offset to apply after global merge.\\n    pub offset: usize,\\n\\n    /// Limit to apply after global merge.\\n    pub limit: usize,\\n\\n    /// Whether the client requested ranking scores in the response.\\n    pub client_requested_score: bool,\\n\\n    /// Facet names to merge (if None, merge all facets).\\n    pub facets: Option<Vec<String>>,\\n}\\n\\n/// Merged search result.\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\\npub struct MergedSearchResult {\\n    /// Merged hits (globally sorted, offset/limit applied).\\n    pub hits: Vec<Value>,\\n\\n    /// Aggregated facets.\\n    pub facets: Value,\\n\\n    /// Estimated total hits (sum of shard totals).\\n    pub estimated_total_hits: u64,\\n\\n    /// Processing time in milliseconds (max across shards).\\n    pub processing_time_ms: u64,\\n\\n    /// Whether the response is degraded (some shards failed).\\n    pub degraded: bool,\\n}\\n\\n/// Scored hit for heap-based top-k selection.\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\\nstruct ScoredHit {\\n    /// Ranking score (negated for min-heap as max-heap).\\n    score: f64,\\n\\n    /// Primary key for tie-breaking (negated for reverse ordering).\\n    primary_key: String,\\n\\n    /// The hit document.\\n    hit: Value,\\n}\\n\\n// Implement Ord for BinaryHeap (max-heap behavior via negated scores)\\nimpl PartialEq for ScoredHit {\\n    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {\\n        self.score == other.score && self.primary_key == other.primary_key\\n    }\\n}\\n\\nimpl Eq for ScoredHit {}\\n\\n// BinaryHeap is a max-heap, but we want min-heap behavior for top-k\\n// We negate scores to get the smallest (worst) at the top\\nimpl PartialOrd for ScoredHit {\\n    fn partial_cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Option<Ordering> {\\n        Some(self.cmp(other))\\n    }\\n}\\n\\nimpl Ord for ScoredHit {\\n    fn cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Ordering {\\n        // First compare by score (higher scores are \\\"better\\\" and should come first)\\n        // Since we're using a min-heap to track the k-best, we negate\\n        match self.score.partial_cmp(&other.score) {\\n            Some(Ordering::Equal) => {}\\n            Some(ord) => return ord,\\n            None => {\\n                // NaN handling: treat NaN as worse than any finite score\\n                if self.score.is_nan() {\\n                    return Ordering::Less;\\n                }\\n                if other.score.is_nan() {\\n                    return Ordering::Greater;\\n                }\\n            }\\n        }\\n        // Tie-break: lexicographic primary_key (reversed for min-heap)\\n        self.primary_key.cmp(&other.primary_key)\\n    }\\n}\\n\\n/// Merge search results from multiple shards.\\n///\\n/// This is a pure function — testable without a network — and produces\\n/// deterministic, byte-identical JSON for the same input.\\n///\\n/// # Algorithm\\n///\\n/// 1. Collect all hits with scores from all successful shards\\n/// 2. Use a binary min-heap of size `offset + limit` to efficiently find top-k\\n/// 3. Sort the top-k by score descending (with tie-breaking)\\n/// 4. Apply offset and limit\\n/// 5. Strip `_rankingScore` if not requested by client\\n/// 6. Strip `_miroir_shard` (always removed)\\n/// 7. Merge facet counts using BTreeMap for stable ordering\\n/// 8. Sum `estimatedTotalHits` across shards\\n/// 9. Take max `processingTimeMs` across shards\\n///\\n/// # Arguments\\n///\\n/// * `input` - Merge parameters including shard responses and pagination settings\\n///\\n/// # Returns\\n///\\n/// A merged search result with globally sorted hits and aggregated metadata.\\npub fn merge(input: MergeInput) -> MergedSearchResult {\\n    // Filter to only successful responses\\n    let successful_shards: Vec<_> = input\\n        .shard_hits\\n        .iter()\\n        .filter(|s| s.success)\\n        .collect();\\n\\n    // Check if any shards failed (degraded mode)\\n    let degraded = successful_shards.len() < input.shard_hits.len();\\n\\n    // Early return for empty successful shards\\n    if successful_shards.is_empty() {\\n        return MergedSearchResult {\\n            hits: vec![],\\n            facets: serde_json::json!({}),\\n            estimated_total_hits: 0,\\n            processing_time_ms: 0,\\n            degraded,\\n        };\\n    }\\n\\n    // Use min-heap for efficient top-k selection when fan-out is large\\n    let heap_size = input.offset + input.limit;\\n    let mut heap = BinaryHeap::new();\\n\\n    for shard in &successful_shards {\\n        if let Some(hits) = shard.body.get(\\\"hits\\\").and_then(|h| h.as_array()) {\\n            for hit in hits {\\n                // Extract ranking score\\n                let score = hit\\n                    .get(\\\"_rankingScore\\\")\\n                    .and_then(|s| s.as_f64())\\n                    .unwrap_or(0.0);\\n\\n                // Extract primary key for tie-breaking\\n                let primary_key = hit\\n                    .get(\\\"id\\\")\\n                    .and_then(|id| id.as_str())\\n                    .unwrap_or(\\\"\\\")\\n                    .to_string();\\n\\n                // Negate score for min-heap behavior (BinaryHeap is max-heap)\\n                let scored_hit = ScoredHit {\\n                    score: -score, // Negate for min-heap as max-heap\\n                    primary_key,\\n                    hit: hit.clone(),\\n                };\\n\\n                heap.push(scored_hit);\\n\\n                // Keep only top heap_size elements\\n                if heap.len() > heap_size {\\n                    heap.pop();\\n                }\\n            }\\n        }\\n    }\\n\\n    // Convert heap to sorted vector\\n    let mut sorted_hits: Vec<ScoredHit> = heap.into_iter().collect();\\n    sorted_hits.sort_by(|a, b| {\\n        // Compare by score descending (remember scores are negated)\\n        match a.score.partial_cmp(&b.score) {\\n            Some(Ordering::Equal) => {}\\n            Some(ord) => return ord.reverse(),\\n            None => {\\n                if a.score.is_nan() {\\n                    return Ordering::Greater;\\n                }\\n                if b.score.is_nan() {\\n                    return Ordering::Less;\\n                }\\n            }\\n        }\\n        // Tie-break by primary_key ascending (also reversed due to negation)\\n        a.primary_key.cmp(&b.primary_key).reverse()\\n    });\\n\\n    // Apply offset and limit\\n    let hits: Vec<Value> = sorted_hits\\n        .into_iter()\\n        .skip(input.offset)\\n        .take(input.limit)\\n        .map(|mut scored_hit| {\\n            let hit = &mut scored_hit.hit;\\n\\n            // Strip _miroir_shard (always removed)\\n            if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\\n                obj.remove(\\\"_miroir_shard\\\");\\n            }\\n\\n            // Strip _rankingScore if client didn't request it\\n            if !input.client_requested_score {\\n                if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\\n                    obj.remove(\\\"_rankingScore\\\");\\n                }\\n            }\\n\\n            hit.clone()\\n        })\\n        .collect();\\n\\n    // Merge facets using BTreeMap for stable ordering\\n    let facets = merge_facets(&successful_shards, input.facets.as_deref());\\n\\n    // Sum estimated total hits\\n    let estimated_total_hits: u64 = successful_shards\\n        .iter()\\n        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\\\"estimatedTotalHits\\\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\\n        .sum();\\n\\n    // Max processing time across all shards\\n    let processing_time_ms: u64 = successful_shards\\n        .iter()\\n        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\\\"processingTimeMs\\\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\\n        .max()\\n        .unwrap_or(0);\\n\\n    MergedSearchResult {\\n        hits,\\n        facets,\\n        estimated_total_hits,\\n        processing_time_ms,\\n        degraded,\\n    }\\n}\\n\\n/// Merge facet distributions from all shards.\\n///\\n/// Uses BTreeMap for deterministic ordering — the same input produces\\n/// byte-identical JSON output, which is critical for the compatibility suite.\\n///\\n/// Facets are nested objects like `{\\\"color\\\": {\\\"red\\\": 10, \\\"blue\\\": 5}}`.\\n/// We sum counts for each facet value across all shards.\\nfn merge_facets(\\n    shards: &[&ShardHitPage],\\n    facet_filter: Option<&[String]>,\\n) -> Value {\\n    let mut merged_facets: BTreeMap<String, BTreeMap<String, u64>> = BTreeMap::new();\\n\\n    for shard in shards {\\n        if let Some(facets) = shard\\n            .body\\n            .get(\\\"facetDistribution\\\")\\n            .and_then(|f| f.as_object())\\n        {\\n            for (facet_name, facet_values) in facets {\\n                // Skip if facet filter is set and this facet is not in it\\n                if let Some(filter) = facet_filter {\\n                    if !filter.contains(&facet_name) {\\n                        continue;\\n                    }\\n                }\\n\\n                if let Some(values_obj) = facet_values.as_object() {\\n                    let entry = merged_facets.entry(facet_name.clone()).or_default();\\n\\n                    for (value, count) in values_obj {\\n                        let count_val = count.as_u64().unwrap_or(0);\\n                        *entry.entry(value.clone()).or_insert(0) += count_val;\\n                    }\\n                }\\n            }\\n        }\\n    }\\n\\n    // Convert back to JSON structure (BTreeMap ensures stable ordering)\\n    let mut result = serde_json::Map::new();\\n    for (facet_name, values) in merged_facets {\\n        let values_obj: serde_json::Map<String, Value> = values\\n            .into_iter()\\n            .map(|(k, v)| (k, Value::Number(v.into())))\\n            .collect();\\n        result.insert(facet_name, Value::Object(values_obj));\\n    }\\n\\n    Value::Object(result)\\n}\\n\\n/// Legacy trait-based API for backward compatibility.\\n/// New code should use the `merge` function directly.\\npub trait Merger: Send + Sync {\\n    /// Merge search results from multiple shards.\\n    fn merge(\\n        &self,\\n        shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\\n        offset: usize,\\n        limit: usize,\\n        client_requested_score: bool,\\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult>;\\n}\\n\\n/// Response from a single shard (legacy type).\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\\npub struct ShardResponse {\\n    /// Shard identifier.\\n    pub shard_id: u32,\\n\\n    /// Raw JSON response from the node.\\n    pub body: Value,\\n\\n    /// Whether this shard succeeded.\\n    pub success: bool,\\n}\\n\\n/// Merged search result (legacy type).\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\\npub struct MergedResult {\\n    /// Merged hits (globally sorted, offset/limit applied).\\n    pub hits: Vec<Value>,\\n\\n    /// Aggregated facets.\\n    pub facets: Value,\\n\\n    /// Estimated total hits (sum of shard totals).\\n    pub total_hits: u64,\\n\\n    /// Processing time in milliseconds.\\n    pub processing_time_ms: u64,\\n\\n    /// Whether the response is degraded (some shards failed).\\n    pub degraded: bool,\\n}\\n\\n/// Default implementation of Merger (legacy wrapper).\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\\npub struct MergerImpl;\\n\\nimpl Merger for MergerImpl {\\n    fn merge(\\n        &self,\\n        shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\\n        offset: usize,\\n        limit: usize,\\n        client_requested_score: bool,\\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult> {\\n        let shard_hits: Vec<ShardHitPage> = shard_responses\\n            .into_iter()\\n            .map(|sr| ShardHitPage {\\n                body: sr.body,\\n                success: sr.success,\\n            })\\n            .collect();\\n\\n        let input = MergeInput {\\n            shard_hits,\\n            offset,\\n            limit,\\n            client_requested_score,\\n            facets: None,\\n        };\\n\\n        let result = merge(input);\\n\\n        Ok(MergedResult {\\n            hits: result.hits,\\n            facets: result.facets,\\n            total_hits: result.estimated_total_hits,\\n            processing_time_ms: result.processing_time_ms,\\n            degraded: result.degraded,\\n        })\\n    }\\n}\\n\\n/// Stub implementation that returns empty results (legacy).\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\\npub struct StubMerger;\\n\\nimpl Merger for StubMerger {\\n    fn merge(\\n        &self,\\n        _shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\\n        _offset: usize,\\n        _limit: usize,\\n        _client_requested_score: bool,\\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult> {\\n        Ok(MergedResult {\\n            hits: Vec::new(),\\n            facets: serde_json::json!({}),\\n            total_hits: 0,\\n            processing_time_ms: 0,\\n            degraded: false,\\n        })\\n    }\\n}\\n\\n#[cfg(test)]\\nmod tests {\\n    use super::*;\\n\\n    fn create_hit(score: f64, id: &str) -> Value {\\n        serde_json::json!({\\n            \\\"id\\\": id,\\n            \\\"_rankingScore\\\": score,\\n            \\\"_miroir_shard\\\": 0,\\n        })\\n    }\\n\\n    fn create_shard_page(hits: Vec<Value>, total: u64) -> ShardHitPage {\\n        ShardHitPage {\\n            body: serde_json::json!({\\n                \\\"hits\\\": hits,\\n                \\\"estimatedTotalHits\\\": total,\\n                \\\"processingTimeMs\\\": 10,\\n                \\\"facetDistribution\\\": {},\\n            }),\\n            success: true,\\n        }\\n    }\\n\\n    fn create_shard_page_with_facets(\\n        hits: Vec<Value>,\\n        total: u64,\\n        facets: Value,\\n    ) -> ShardHitPage {\\n        ShardHitPage {\\n            body: serde_json::json!({\\n                \\\"hits\\\": hits,\\n                \\\"estimatedTotalHits\\\": total,\\n                \\\"processingTimeMs\\\": 10,\\n                \\\"facetDistribution\\\": facets,\\n            }),\\n            success: true,\\n        }\\n    }\\n\\n    #[test]\\n    fn test_stable_serialization_same_input_same_json() {\\n        let facets1 = serde_json::json!({\\n            \\\"color\\\": {\\\"red\\\": 10, \\\"blue\\\": 5},\\n            \\\"size\\\": {\\\"large\\\": 8}\\n        });\\n\\n        let facets2 = serde_json::json!({\\n            \\\"color\\\": {\\\"red\\\": 7, \\\"green\\\": 3},\\n            \\\"size\\\": {\\\"large\\\": 4, \\\"small\\\": 6}\\n        });\\n\\n        let input = MergeInput {\\n            shard_hits: vec![\\n                create_shard_page_with_facets(vec![], 0, facets1),\\n                create_shard_page_with_facets(vec![], 0, facets2),\\n            ],\\n            offset: 0,\\n            limit: 10,\\n            client_requested_score: false,\\n            facets: None,\\n Result merger: combines shard results into a single response.\n\nuse crate::Result;\nuse serde_json::Value;\nuse std::collections::{BTreeMap, BinaryHeap};\nuse std::cmp::Ordering;\n\n/// A single page of hits from a shard.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ShardHitPage {\n    /// Raw JSON response from the shard.\n    pub body: Value,\n\n    /// Whether this shard succeeded.\n    pub success: bool,\n}\n\n/// Input to the merge function.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MergeInput {\n    /// One page per node in the covering set.\n    pub shard_hits: Vec<ShardHitPage>,\n\n    /// Offset to apply after global merge.\n    pub offset: usize,\n\n    /// Limit to apply after global merge.\n    pub limit: usize,\n\n    /// Whether the client requested ranking scores in the response.\n    pub client_requested_score: bool,\n\n    /// Facet names to merge (if None, merge all facets).\n    pub facets: Option<Vec<String>>,\n}\n\n/// Merged search result.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MergedSearchResult {\n    /// Merged hits (globally sorted, offset/limit applied).\n    pub hits: Vec<Value>,\n\n    /// Aggregated facets.\n    pub facets: Value,\n\n    /// Estimated total hits (sum of shard totals).\n    pub estimated_total_hits: u64,\n\n    /// Processing time in milliseconds (max across shards).\n    pub processing_time_ms: u64,\n\n    /// Whether the response is degraded (some shards failed).\n    pub degraded: bool,\n}\n\n/// Scored hit for heap-based top-k selection.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\nstruct ScoredHit {\n    /// Ranking score (negated for min-heap as max-heap).\n    score: f64,\n\n    /// Primary key for tie-breaking (negated for reverse ordering).\n    primary_key: String,\n\n    /// The hit document.\n    hit: Value,\n}\n\n// Implement Ord for BinaryHeap (max-heap behavior via negated scores)\nimpl PartialEq for ScoredHit {\n    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {\n        self.score == other.score && self.primary_key == other.primary_key\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Eq for ScoredHit {}\n\n// BinaryHeap is a max-heap, but we want min-heap behavior for top-k\n// We negate scores to get the smallest (worst) at the top\nimpl PartialOrd for ScoredHit {\n    fn partial_cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Option<Ordering> {\n        Some(self.cmp(other))\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Ord for ScoredHit {\n    fn cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Ordering {\n        // First compare by score (higher scores are \"better\" and should come first)\n        // Since we're using a min-heap to track the k-best, we negate\n        match self.score.partial_cmp(&other.score) {\n            Some(Ordering::Equal) => {}\n            Some(ord) => return ord,\n            None => {\n                // NaN handling: treat NaN as worse than any finite score\n                if self.score.is_nan() {\n                    return Ordering::Less;\n                }\n                if other.score.is_nan() {\n                    return Ordering::Greater;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        // Tie-break: lexicographic primary_key (reversed for min-heap)\n        self.primary_key.cmp(&other.primary_key)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Merge search results from multiple shards.\n///\n/// This is a pure function — testable without a network — and produces\n/// deterministic, byte-identical JSON for the same input.\n///\n/// # Algorithm\n///\n/// 1. Collect all hits with scores from all successful shards\n/// 2. Use a binary min-heap of size `offset + limit` to efficiently find top-k\n/// 3. Sort the top-k by score descending (with tie-breaking)\n/// 4. Apply offset and limit\n/// 5. Strip `_rankingScore` if not requested by client\n/// 6. Strip `_miroir_shard` (always removed)\n/// 7. Merge facet counts using BTreeMap for stable ordering\n/// 8. Sum `estimatedTotalHits` across shards\n/// 9. Take max `processingTimeMs` across shards\n///\n/// # Arguments\n///\n/// * `input` - Merge parameters including shard responses and pagination settings\n///\n/// # Returns\n///\n/// A merged search result with globally sorted hits and aggregated metadata.\npub fn merge(input: MergeInput) -> MergedSearchResult {\n    // Filter to only successful responses\n    let successful_shards: Vec<_> = input\n        .shard_hits\n        .iter()\n        .filter(|s| s.success)\n        .collect();\n\n    // Check if any shards failed (degraded mode)\n    let degraded = successful_shards.len() < input.shard_hits.len();\n\n    // Early return for empty successful shards\n    if successful_shards.is_empty() {\n        return MergedSearchResult {\n            hits: vec![],\n            facets: serde_json::json!({}),\n            estimated_total_hits: 0,\n            processing_time_ms: 0,\n            degraded,\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Use min-heap for efficient top-k selection when fan-out is large\n    let heap_size = input.offset + input.limit;\n    let mut heap = BinaryHeap::new();\n\n    for shard in &successful_shards {\n        if let Some(hits) = shard.body.get(\"hits\").and_then(|h| h.as_array()) {\n            for hit in hits {\n                // Extract ranking score\n                let score = hit\n                    .get(\"_rankingScore\")\n                    .and_then(|s| s.as_f64())\n                    .unwrap_or(0.0);\n\n                // Extract primary key for tie-breaking\n                let primary_key = hit\n                    .get(\"id\")\n                    .and_then(|id| id.as_str())\n                    .unwrap_or(\"\")\n                    .to_string();\n\n                // Negate score for min-heap behavior (BinaryHeap is max-heap)\n                let scored_hit = ScoredHit {\n                    score: -score, // Negate for min-heap as max-heap\n                    primary_key,\n                    hit: hit.clone(),\n                };\n\n                heap.push(scored_hit);\n\n                // Keep only top heap_size elements\n                if heap.len() > heap_size {\n                    heap.pop();\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Convert heap to sorted vector\n    let mut sorted_hits: Vec<ScoredHit> = heap.into_iter().collect();\n    sorted_hits.sort_by(|a, b| {\n        // Compare by score descending (remember scores are negated)\n        match a.score.partial_cmp(&b.score) {\n            Some(Ordering::Equal) => {}\n            Some(ord) => return ord.reverse(),\n            None => {\n                if a.score.is_nan() {\n                    return Ordering::Greater;\n                }\n                if b.score.is_nan() {\n                    return Ordering::Less;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        // Tie-break by primary_key ascending (also reversed due to negation)\n        a.primary_key.cmp(&b.primary_key).reverse()\n    });\n\n    // Apply offset and limit\n    let hits: Vec<Value> = sorted_hits\n        .into_iter()\n        .skip(input.offset)\n        .take(input.limit)\n        .map(|mut scored_hit| {\n            let hit = &mut scored_hit.hit;\n\n            // Strip _miroir_shard (always removed)\n            if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\n                obj.remove(\"_miroir_shard\");\n            }\n\n            // Strip _rankingScore if client didn't request it\n            if !input.client_requested_score {\n                if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\n                    obj.remove(\"_rankingScore\");\n                }\n            }\n\n            hit.clone()\n        })\n        .collect();\n\n    // Merge facets using BTreeMap for stable ordering\n    let facets = merge_facets(&successful_shards, input.facets.as_deref());\n\n    // Sum estimated total hits\n    let estimated_total_hits: u64 = successful_shards\n        .iter()\n        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\"estimatedTotalHits\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\n        .sum();\n\n    // Max processing time across all shards\n    let processing_time_ms: u64 = successful_shards\n        .iter()\n        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\"processingTimeMs\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\n        .max()\n        .unwrap_or(0);\n\n    MergedSearchResult {\n        hits,\n        facets,\n        estimated_total_hits,\n        processing_time_ms,\n        degraded,\n    }\n}\n\n/// Merge facet distributions from all shards.\n///\n/// Uses BTreeMap for deterministic ordering — the same input produces\n/// byte-identical JSON output, which is critical for the compatibility suite.\n///\n/// Facets are nested objects like `{\"color\": {\"red\": 10, \"blue\": 5}}`.\n/// We sum counts for each facet value across all shards.\nfn merge_facets(\n    shards: &[&ShardHitPage],\n    facet_filter: Option<&[String]>,\n) -> Value {\n    let mut merged_facets: BTreeMap<String, BTreeMap<String, u64>> = BTreeMap::new();\n\n    for shard in shards {\n        if let Some(facets) = shard\n            .body\n            .get(\"facetDistribution\")\n            .and_then(|f| f.as_object())\n        {\n            for (facet_name, facet_values) in facets {\n                // Skip if facet filter is set and this facet is not in it\n                if let Some(filter) = facet_filter {\n                    if !filter.contains(&facet_name) {\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if let Some(values_obj) = facet_values.as_object() {\n                    let entry = merged_facets.entry(facet_name.clone()).or_default();\n\n                    for (value, count) in values_obj {\n                        let count_val = count.as_u64().unwrap_or(0);\n                        *entry.entry(value.clone()).or_insert(0) += count_val;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Convert back to JSON structure (BTreeMap ensures stable ordering)\n    let mut result = serde_json::Map::new();\n    for (facet_name, values) in merged_facets {\n        let values_obj: serde_json::Map<String, Value> = values\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(|(k, v)| (k, Value::Number(v.into())))\n            .collect();\n        result.insert(facet_name, Value::Object(values_obj));\n    }\n\n    Value::Object(result)\n}\n\n/// Legacy trait-based API for backward compatibility.\n/// New code should use the `merge` function directly.\npub trait Merger: Send + Sync {\n    /// Merge search results from multiple shards.\n    fn merge(\n        &self,\n        shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n        offset: usize,\n        limit: usize,\n        client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult>;\n}\n\n/// Response from a single shard (legacy type).\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult> {\n        let shard_hits: Vec<ShardHitPage> = shard_responses\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(|sr| ShardHitPage {\n                body: sr.body,\n                success: sr.success,\n            })\n            .collect();\n\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits,\n            offset,\n facets: result.facets,\n            total_hits: result.estimated_total_hits,\n            processing_time_ms: result.processing_time_ms,\n            degraded: result.degraded,\n        })\n Strips `_rankingScore` if client didn't request it\n62\t/// 5. Always strips `_miroir_*` reserved fields\n63\t/// 6. Sums facet counts across shards\n64\t/// 7. Sums `estimatedTotalHits` across shards\n65\t/// 8. Takes max `processingTimeMs` across shards\n66\t///\n67\t/// Uses a binary min-heap to avoid keeping all hits in RAM when fan-out is large.\n68\t/// Uses BTreeMap for stable facet serialization (deterministic JSON output).\n69\tpub fn merge(input: MergeInput) -> MergedSearchResult {\n70\t    // Filter to only successful responses\n71\t    let successful_shards: Vec<_> = input\n72\t        .shard_hits\n73\t        .iter()\n74\t        .filter(|s| s.success)\n75\t        .collect();\n76\t\n77\t    // Check if any shards failed (degraded mode)\n78\t    let degraded = successful_shards.len() < input.shard_hits.len();\n79\t\n80\t    // Collect all hits with their ranking scores and primary keys\n81\t    let mut all_hits: Vec<HitWithScore> = Vec::new();\n82\t\n83\t    for shard in &successful_shards {\n84\t        if let Some(hits) = shard.body.get(\"hits\").and_then(|h| h.as_array()) {\n85\t            for hit in hits {\n86\t                let score = hit\n87\t                    .get(\"_rankingScore\")\n88\t                    .and_then(|s| s.as_f64())\n89\t                    .unwrap_or(0.0);\n90\t\n91\t                let primary_key = hit\n92\t                    .get(\"id\")\n93\t                    .and_then(|id| id.as_str())\n94\t                    .unwrap_or(\"\")\n95\t                    .to_string();\n96\t\n97\t                all_hits.push(HitWithScore {\n98\t                    score,\n99\t                    primary_key,\n100\t                    hit: hit.clone(),\n101\t                });\n102\t            }\n103\t        }\n104\t    }\n105\t\n106\t    // Use a min-heap of size offset + limit to avoid keeping all hits in RAM\n107\t    let heap_size = input.offset + input.limit;\n108\t    let top_hits = if all_hits.len() > heap_size * 2 {\n109\t        // Only use heap optimization if we have significantly more hits than needed\n110\t        let mut heap = BinaryHeap::new();\n111\t        let heap_capacity = heap_size + 1; // +1 for the pop below\n112\t\n113\t        for hit in all_hits {\n114\t            if heap.len() < heap_capacity {\n115\t                heap.push(hit);\n116\t            } else {\n117\t                // BinaryHeap is a max-heap, but we want a min-heap for top-K\n118\t                // So we push and then pop the smallest if we're over capacity\n119\t                if let Some(mut smallest) = heap.peek() {\n120\t                    if hit > *smallest {\n121\t                        heap.pop();\n122\t                        heap.push(hit);\n123\t                    }\n124\t                }\n125\t            }\n126\t        }\n127\t\n128\t        // Convert to sorted vector (descending by score)\n129\t        let mut result: Vec<_> = heap.into_iter().collect();\n130\t        result.sort_by(|a, b| b.cmp(a));\n131\t        result\n132\t    } else {\n133\t        // For smaller result sets, just sort directly\n134\t        all_hits.sort_by(|a, b| b.cmp(a));\n135\t        all_hits\n136\t    };\n137\t\n138\t    // Apply offset and limit\n139\t    let page: Vec<Value> = top_hits\n140\t        .into_iter()\n141\t        .skip(input.offset)\n142\t        .take(input.limit)\n143\t        .map(|mut hit_with_score| {\n144\t            let hit = &mut hit_with_score.hit;\n145\t\n146\t            // Strip all _miroir_* fields (always removed)\n147\t            if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\n148\t                obj.retain(|k, _| !k.starts_with(\"_miroir_\"));\n149\t            }\n150\t\n151\t            // Strip _rankingScore if client didn't request it\n152\t            if !input.client_requested_score {\n153\t                if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\n154\t                    obj.remove(\"_rankingScore\");\n155\t                }\n156\t            }\n157\t\n158\t            hit.clone()\n159\t        })\n160\t        .collect();\n161\t\n162\t    // Aggregate facets across all shards\n163\t    let facets = merge_facets(&successful_shards, input.facets.as_deref());\n164\t\n165\t    // Sum estimated total hits\n166\t    let estimated_total_hits: u64 = successful_shards\n167\t        .iter()\n168\t        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\"estimatedTotalHits\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\n169\t        .sum();\n170\t\n171\t    // Max processing time across all shards\n172\t    let processing_time_ms: u64 = successful_shards\n173\t        .iter()\n174\t        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\"processingTimeMs\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\n175\t        .max()\n176\t        .unwrap_or(0);\n177\t\n178\t    MergedSearchResult {\n179\t        hits: page,\n180\t        facets,\n181\t        estimated_total_hits,\n182\t        processing_time_ms,\n183\t        degraded,\n184\t    }\n185\t}\n186\t\n187\t/// A hit with its ranking score for sorting.\n188\t#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\n189\tstruct HitWithScore {\n190\t    score: f64,\n191\t    primary_key: String,\n192\t    hit: Value,\n193\t}\n194\t\n195\timpl PartialEq for HitWithScore {\n196\t    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {\n197\t        self.score == other.score && self.primary_key == other.primary_key\n198\t    }\n199\t}\n200\t\n201\timpl Eq for HitWithScore {}\n202\t\n203\timpl PartialOrd for HitWithScore {\n204\t    fn partial_cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Option<std::cmp::Ordering> {\n205\t        Some(self.cmp(other))\n206\t    }\n207\t}\n208\t\n209\timpl Ord for HitWithScore {\n210\t    fn cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> std::cmp::Ordering {\n211\t        // Sort by score descending, then by primary key ascending for tie-breaking\n212\t        match self.score.partial_cmp(&other.score) {\n213\t            Some(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal) | None => {\n214\t                // On equal scores (or NaN), fall back to primary key\n215\t                // Reversed for descending order\n216\t                other.primary_key.cmp(&self.primary_key)\n217\t            }\n218\t            Some(ord) => ord.reverse(),\n219\t        }\n220\t    }\n221\t}\n222\t\n223\t/// Result merger: combines responses from multiple shards.\n224\tpub trait Merger: Send + Sync {\n225\t    /// Merge search results from multiple shards.\n226\t    ///\n227\t    /// Takes the raw JSON responses from each shard and produces\n228\t    /// a merged result with global sorting, offset/limit applied,\n229\t    /// and facet aggregation.\n230\t    fn merge(\n231\t        &self,\n232\t        shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n233\t        offset: usize,\n234\t        limit: usize,\n235\t        client_requested_score: bool,\n236\t    ) -> Result<MergedResult>;\n237\t}\n238\t\n239\t/// Response from a single shard.\n240\t#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\n241\tpub struct ShardResponse {\n242\t    /// Shard identifier.\n243\t    pub shard_id: u32,\n244\t\n245\t    /// Raw JSON response from the node.\n246\t    pub body: Value,\n247\t\n248\t    /// Whether this shard succeeded.\n249\t    pub success: bool,\n250\t}\n251\t\n252\t/// Merged search result (legacy, use MergedSearchResult instead).\n253\t#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\n254\tpub struct MergedResult {\n255\t    /// Merged hits (globally sorted, offset/limit applied).\n256\t    pub hits: Vec<Value>,\n257\t\n258\t    /// Aggregated facets.\n259\t    pub facets: Value,\n260\t\n261\t    /// Estimated total hits (sum of shard totals).\n262\t    pub total_hits: u64,\n263\t\n264\t    /// Processing time in milliseconds.\n265\t    pub processing_time_ms: u64,\n266\t\n267\t    /// Whether the response is degraded (some shards failed).\n268\t    pub degraded: bool,\n269\t}\n270\t\n271\t/// Default implementation of Merger.\n272\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\n273\tpub struct MergerImpl;\n274\t\n275\timpl Merger for MergerImpl {\n276\t    fn merge(\n277\t        &self,\n278\t        shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n279\t        offset: usize,\n280\t        limit: usize,\n281\t        client_requested_score: bool,\n282\t    ) -> Result<MergedResult> {\n283\t        // Convert ShardResponse to ShardHitPage\n284\t        let shard_hits: Vec<ShardHitPage> = shard_responses\n285\t            .into_iter()\n286\t            .map(|sr| ShardHitPage {\n287\t                body: sr.body,\n288\t                success: sr.success,\n289\t            })\n290\t            .collect();\n291\t\n292\t        // Call the new merge function\n293\t        let input = MergeInput {\n294\t            shard_hits,\n295\t            offset,\n296\t            limit,\n297\t            client_requested_score,\n298\t            facets: None,\n299\t        };\n300\t\n301\t        let result = merge(input);\n302\t\n303\t        Ok(MergedResult {\n304\t            hits: result.hits,\n305\t            facets: result.facets,\n306\t            total_hits: result.estimated_total_hits,\n307\t            processing_time_ms: result.processing_time_ms,\n308\t            degraded: result.degraded,\n309\t        })\n310\t    }\n311\t}\n312\t\n313\t/// Merge facet distributions from all shards.\n314\t///\n315\t/// Facets are nested objects like `{\"color\": {\"red\": 10, \"blue\": 5}}`.\n316\t/// We sum counts for each facet value across all shards.\n317\t///\n318\t/// Uses BTreeMap for stable, deterministic serialization.\n319\tfn merge_facets(shards: &[&ShardHitPage], facet_filter: Option<&[String]>) -> Value {\n320\t    let mut merged_facets: BTreeMap<String, BTreeMap<String, u64>> = BTreeMap::new();\n321\t\n322\t    for shard in shards {\n323\t        if let Some(facets) = shard\n324\t            .body\n325\t            .get(\"facetDistribution\")\n326\t            .and_then(|f| f.as_object())\n327\t        {\n328\t            for (facet_name, facet_values) in facets {\n329\t                // Apply facet filter if provided\n330\t                if let Some(filter) = facet_filter {\n331\t                    if !filter.contains(&facet_name) {\n332\t                        continue;\n333\t                    }\n334\t                }\n335\t\n336\t                if let Some(values_obj) = facet_values.as_object() {\n337\t                    let entry = merged_facets.entry(facet_name.clone()).or_default();\n338\t\n339\t                    for (value, count) in values_obj {\n340\t                        let count_val = count.as_u64().unwrap_or(0);\n341\t                        *entry.entry(value.clone()).or_insert(0) += count_val;\n342\t                    }\n343\t                }\n344\t            }\n345\t        }\n346\t    }\n347\t\n348\t    // Convert back to JSON structure (BTreeMap ensures stable key order)\n349\t    let result: serde_json::Map<String, Value> = merged_facets\n350\t        .into_iter()\n351\t        .map(|(facet_name, values)| {\n352\t            let values_obj: serde_json::Map<String, Value> = values\n353\t                .into_iter()\n354\t                .map(|(k, v)| (k, Value::Number(v.into())))\n355\t                .collect();\n356\t            (facet_name, Value::Object(values_obj))\n357\t        })\n358\t        .collect();\n359\t\n360\t    Value::Object(result)\n361\t}\n362\t\n363\t/// Stub implementation that returns empty results.\n364\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\n365\tpub struct StubMerger;\n366\t\n367\timpl Merger for StubMerger {\n368\t    fn merge(\n369\t        &self,\n370\t        _shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n371\t        _offset: usize,\n372\t        _limit: usize,\n373\t        _client_requested_score: bool,\n374\t    ) -> Result<MergedResult> {\n375\t        Ok(MergedResult {\n376\t            hits: Vec::new(),\n377\t            facets: serde_json::json!({}),\n378\t            total_hits: 0,\n379\t            processing_time_ms: 0,\n380\t            degraded: false,\n381\t        })\n382\t    }\n383\t}\n384\t\n385\t#[cfg(test)]\n386\tmod tests {\n387\t    use super::*;\n388\t\n389\t    fn create_hit(score: f64, id: &str) -> Value {\n390\t        serde_json::json!({\n391\t }\n408\t    }\n409\t\n410\t    #[test]\n411\t    fn test_global_sort_by_ranking_score() {\n412\t        let merger = MergerImpl;\n413\t\n414\t        let hits1 = vec![\n415\t Result merger: combines shard results into a single response.\n\nuse crate::Result;\nuse serde_json::Value;\nuse std::collections::{BTreeMap, BinaryHeap};\n\n/// Input to the merge function.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MergeInput {\n    /// One page of hits per node in the covering set.\n    pub shard_hits: Vec<ShardHitPage>,\n\n    /// Offset to apply after merge.\n    pub offset: usize,\n\n    /// Limit to apply after merge.\n    pub limit: usize,\n\n    /// Whether the client requested the ranking score in the response.\n    pub client_requested_score: bool,\n\n    /// Facet names to include (if None, include all).\n    pub facets: Option<Vec<String>>,\n}\n\n/// A page of hits from a single shard.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ShardHitPage {\n    /// Raw JSON response from the node.\n    pub body: Value,\n\n    /// Whether this shard succeeded.\n    pub success: bool,\n}\n\n/// Merged search result.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MergedSearchResult {\n    /// Merged hits (globally sorted, offset/limit applied).\n    pub hits: Vec<Value>,\n\n    /// Aggregated facets.\n    pub facets: Value,\n\n    /// Estimated total hits (sum of shard totals).\n    pub estimated_total_hits: u64,\n\n    /// Processing time in milliseconds.\n    pub processing_time_ms: u64,\n\n    /// Whether the response is degraded (some shards failed).\n    pub degraded: bool,\n}\n\n/// Merge search results from multiple shards.\n///\n/// This is the primary entry point for result merging. It:\n/// 1. Collects all hits with scores from all shards\n/// 2. Sorts globally by `_rankingScore` descending\n/// 3. Applies offset + limit after merge\n/// 4. Strips `_rankingScore` if client didn't request it\n/// 5. Always strips `_miroir_*` reserved fields\n/// 6. Sums facet counts across shards\n/// 7. Sums `estimatedTotalHits` across shards\n/// 8. Takes max `processingTimeMs` across shards\n///\n/// Uses a binary min-heap to avoid keeping all hits in RAM when fan-out is large.\n/// Uses BTreeMap for stable facet serialization (deterministic JSON output).\npub fn merge(input: MergeInput) -> MergedSearchResult {\n    // Filter to only successful responses\n    let successful_shards: Vec<_> = input\n        .shard_hits\n        .iter()\n        .filter(|s| s.success)\n        .collect();\n\n    // Check if any shards failed (degraded mode)\n    let degraded = successful_shards.len() < input.shard_hits.len();\n\n    // Collect all hits with their ranking scores and primary keys\n    let mut all_hits: Vec<HitWithScore> = Vec::new();\n\n    for shard in &successful_shards {\n        if let Some(hits) = shard.body.get(\"hits\").and_then(|h| h.as_array()) {\n            for hit in hits {\n                let score = hit\n                    .get(\"_rankingScore\")\n                    .and_then(|s| s.as_f64())\n                    .unwrap_or(0.0);\n\n                let primary_key = hit\n                    .get(\"id\")\n                    .and_then(|id| id.as_str())\n                    .unwrap_or(\"\")\n                    .to_string();\n\n                all_hits.push(HitWithScore {\n                    score,\n                    primary_key,\n                    hit: hit.clone(),\n                });\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Use a min-heap of size offset + limit to avoid keeping all hits in RAM\n    let heap_size = input.offset + input.limit;\n    let top_hits = if all_hits.len() > heap_size * 2 {\n        // Only use heap optimization if we have significantly more hits than needed\n        let mut heap = BinaryHeap::new();\n        let heap_capacity = heap_size + 1; // +1 for the pop below\n\n        for hit in all_hits {\n            if heap.len() < heap_capacity {\n                heap.push(hit);\n            } else {\n                // BinaryHeap is a max-heap, but we want a min-heap for top-K\n                // So we push and then pop the smallest if we're over capacity\n                if let Some(mut smallest) = heap.peek() {\n                    if hit > *smallest {\n                        heap.pop();\n                        heap.push(hit);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Convert to sorted vector (descending by score)\n        let mut result: Vec<_> = heap.into_iter().collect();\n        result.sort_by(|a, b| b.cmp(a));\n        result\n    } else {\n        // For smaller result sets, just sort directly\n        all_hits.sort_by(|a, b| b.cmp(a));\n        all_hits\n    };\n\n    // Apply offset and limit\n    let page: Vec<Value> = top_hits\n        .into_iter()\n        .skip(input.offset)\n        .take(input.limit)\n        .map(|mut hit_with_score| {\n            let hit = &mut hit_with_score.hit;\n\n            // Strip all _miroir_* fields (always removed)\n            if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\n                obj.retain(|k, _| !k.starts_with(\"_miroir_\"));\n            }\n\n            // Strip _rankingScore if client didn't request it\n            if !input.client_requested_score {\n                if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\n                    obj.remove(\"_rankingScore\");\n                }\n            }\n\n            hit.clone()\n        })\n        .collect();\n\n    // Aggregate facets across all shards\n    let facets = merge_facets(&successful_shards, input.facets.as_deref());\n\n    // Sum estimated total hits\n    let estimated_total_hits: u64 = successful_shards\n        .iter()\n        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\"estimatedTotalHits\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\n        .sum();\n\n    // Max processing time across all shards\n    let processing_time_ms: u64 = successful_shards\n        .iter()\n        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\"processingTimeMs\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\n        .max()\n        .unwrap_or(0);\n\n    MergedSearchResult {\n        hits: page,\n        facets,\n        estimated_total_hits,\n        processing_time_ms,\n        degraded,\n    }\n}\n\n/// A hit with its ranking score for sorting.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\nstruct HitWithScore {\n    score: f64,\n    primary_key: String,\n    hit: Value,\n}\n\nimpl PartialEq for HitWithScore {\n    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {\n        self.score == other.score && self.primary_key == other.primary_key\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Eq for HitWithScore {}\n\nimpl PartialOrd for HitWithScore {\n    fn partial_cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Option<std::cmp::Ordering> {\n        Some(self.cmp(other))\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Ord for HitWithScore {\n    fn cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> std::cmp::Ordering {\n        // Sort by score descending, then by primary key ascending for tie-breaking\n        match self.score.partial_cmp(&other.score) {\n            Some(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal) | None => {\n                // On equal scores (or NaN), fall back to primary key\n                // Reversed for descending order\n                other.primary_key.cmp(&self.primary_key)\n            }\n            Some(ord) => ord.reverse(),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Result merger: combines responses from multiple shards.\npub trait Merger: Send + Sync {\n    /// Merge search results from multiple shards.\n    ///\n    /// Takes the raw JSON responses from each shard and produces\n    /// a merged result with global sorting, offset/limit applied,\n    /// and facet aggregation.\n    fn merge(\n        &self,\n        shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n        offset: usize,\n        limit: usize,\n        client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult>;\n}\n\n/// Response from a single shard.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ShardResponse {\n    /// Shard identifier.\n    pub shard_id: u32,\n\n    /// Raw JSON response from the node.\n    pub body: Value,\n\n    /// Whether this shard succeeded.\n    pub success: bool,\n}\n\n/// Merged search result (legacy, use MergedSearchResult instead).\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MergedResult {\n    /// Merged hits (globally sorted, offset/limit applied).\n    pub hits: Vec<Value>,\n\n    /// Aggregated facets.\n    pub facets: Value,\n\n    /// Estimated total hits (sum of shard totals).\n    pub total_hits: u64,\n\n    /// Processing time in milliseconds.\n    pub processing_time_ms: u64,\n\n    /// Whether the response is degraded (some shards failed).\n    pub degraded: bool,\n}\n\n/// Default implementation of Merger.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\npub struct MergerImpl;\n\nimpl Merger for MergerImpl {\n    fn merge(\n        &self,\n        shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n        offset: usize,\n        limit: usize,\n        client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult> {\n        // Convert ShardResponse to ShardHitPage\n        let shard_hits: Vec<ShardHitPage> = shard_responses\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(|sr| ShardHitPage {\n                body: sr.body,\n                success: sr.success,\n            })\n            .collect();\n\n        // Call the new merge function\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits,\n            offset,\n            limit,\n            client_requested_score,\n            facets: None,\n        };\n\n        let result = merge(input);\n\n        Ok(MergedResult {\n            hits: result.hits,\n            facets: result.facets,\n            total_hits: result.estimated_total_hits,\n            processing_time_ms: result.processing_time_ms,\n            degraded: result.degraded,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/// Merge facet distributions from all shards.\n///\n/// Facets are nested objects like `{\"color\": {\"red\": 10, \"blue\": 5}}`.\n/// We sum counts for each facet value across all shards.\n///\n/// Uses BTreeMap for stable, deterministic serialization.\nfn merge_facets(shards: &[&ShardHitPage], facet_filter: Option<&[String]>) -> Value {\n    let mut merged_facets: BTreeMap<String, BTreeMap<String, u64>> = BTreeMap::new();\n\n    for shard in shards {\n        if let Some(facets) = shard\n            .body\n            .get(\"facetDistribution\")\n            .and_then(|f| f.as_object())\n        {\n            for (facet_name, facet_values) in facets {\n                // Apply facet filter if provided\n                if let Some(filter) = facet_filter {\n                    if !filter.contains(&facet_name) {\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if let Some(values_obj) = facet_values.as_object() {\n                    let entry = merged_facets.entry(facet_name.clone()).or_default();\n\n                    for (value, count) in values_obj {\n                        let count_val = count.as_u64().unwrap_or(0);\n                        *entry.entry(value.clone()).or_insert(0) += count_val;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Convert back to JSON structure (BTreeMap ensures stable key order)\n    let result: serde_json::Map<String, Value> = merged_facets\n        .into_iter()\n        .map(|(facet_name, values)| {\n            let values_obj: serde_json::Map<String, Value> = values\n                .into_iter()\n                .map(|(k, v)| (k, Value::Number(v.into())))\n                .collect();\n            (facet_name, Value::Object(values_obj))\n        })\n        .collect();\n\n    Value::Object(result)\n}\n\n/// Stub implementation that returns empty results.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\npub struct StubMerger;\n\nimpl Merger for StubMerger {\n    fn merge(\n        &self,\n        _shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n        _offset: usize,\n        _limit: usize,\n        _client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult> {\n        Ok(MergedResult {\n            hits: Vec::new(),\n            facets: serde_json::json!({}),\n            total_hits: 0,\n            processing_time_ms: 0,\n            degraded: false,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    fn create_hit(score: f64, id: &str) -> Value {\n It:\n/// 1. Collects all hits with scores from all shards\n/// 2. Sorts globally by `_rankingScore` descending\n/// 3. Applies offset + limit after merge\n/// 4. Strips `_rankingScore` if client didn't request it\n/// 5. Always strips `_miroir_*` reserved fields\n/// 6. Sums facet counts across shards\n/// 7. Sums `estimatedTotalHits` across shards\n/// 8. Takes max `processingTimeMs` across shards\n///\n/// Uses a binary min-heap to avoid keeping all hits in RAM when fan-out is large.\n/// Uses BTreeMap for stable facet serialization (deterministic JSON output).\npub fn merge(input: MergeInput) -> MergedSearchResult {\n    // Filter to only successful responses\n    let successful_shards: Vec<_> = input\n        .shard_hits\n        .iter()\n        .filter(|s| s.success)\n        .collect();\n\n    // Check if any shards failed (degraded mode)\n    let degraded = successful_shards.len() < input.shard_hits.len();\n\n    // Collect all hits with their ranking scores and primary keys\n    let mut all_hits: Vec<HitWithScore> = Vec::new();\n\n    for shard in &successful_shards {\n        if let Some(hits) = shard.body.get(\"hits\").and_then(|h| h.as_array()) {\n            for hit in hits {\n                let score = hit\n                    .get(\"_rankingScore\")\n                    .and_then(|s| s.as_f64())\n                    .unwrap_or(0.0);\n\n                let primary_key = hit\n                    .get(\"id\")\n                    .and_then(|id| id.as_str())\n                    .unwrap_or(\"\")\n                    .to_string();\n\n                all_hits.push(HitWithScore {\n                    score,\n                    primary_key,\n                    hit: hit.clone(),\n                });\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Use a min-heap of size offset + limit to avoid keeping all hits in RAM\n    let heap_size = input.offset + input.limit;\n    let top_hits = if all_hits.len() > heap_size * 2 {\n        // Only use heap optimization if we have significantly more hits than needed\n        let mut heap = BinaryHeap::new();\n        let heap_capacity = heap_size + 1; // +1 for the pop below\n\n        for hit in all_hits {\n            if heap.len() < heap_capacity {\n                heap.push(hit);\n            } else {\n                // BinaryHeap is a max-heap, but we want a min-heap for top-K\n                // So we push and then pop the smallest if we're over capacity\n                if let Some(mut smallest) = heap.peek() {\n                    if hit > *smallest {\n                        heap.pop();\n                        heap.push(hit);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Convert to sorted vector (descending by score)\n        let mut result: Vec<_> = heap.into_iter().collect();\n        result.sort_by(|a, b| b.cmp(a));\n        result\n    } else {\n        // For smaller result sets, just sort directly\n        all_hits.sort_by(|a, b| b.cmp(a));\n        all_hits\n    };\n\n    // Apply offset and limit\n    let page: Vec<Value> = top_hits\n        .into_iter()\n        .skip(input.offset)\n        .take(input.limit)\n        .map(|mut hit_with_score| {\n            let hit = &mut hit_with_score.hit;\n\n            // Strip all _miroir_* fields (always removed)\n            if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\n                obj.retain(|k, _| !k.starts_with(\"_miroir_\"));\n            }\n\n            // Strip _rankingScore if client didn't request it\n            if !input.client_requested_score {\n                if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\n                    obj.remove(\"_rankingScore\");\n                }\n            }\n\n            hit.clone()\n        })\n        .collect();\n\n    // Aggregate facets across all shards\n    let facets = merge_facets(&successful_shards, input.facets.as_deref());\n\n    // Sum estimated total hits\n    let estimated_total_hits: u64 = successful_shards\n        .iter()\n        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\"estimatedTotalHits\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\n        .sum();\n\n    // Max processing time across all shards\n    let processing_time_ms: u64 = successful_shards\n        .iter()\n        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\"processingTimeMs\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\n        .max()\n        .unwrap_or(0);\n\n    MergedSearchResult {\n        hits: page,\n        facets,\n        estimated_total_hits,\n        processing_time_ms,\n        degraded,\n    }\n}\n\n/// A hit with its ranking score for sorting.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\nstruct HitWithScore {\n    score: f64,\n    primary_key: String,\n    hit: Value,\n}\n\nimpl PartialEq for HitWithScore {\n    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {\n        self.score == other.score && self.primary_key == other.primary_key\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Eq for HitWithScore {}\n\nimpl PartialOrd for HitWithScore {\n    fn partial_cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Option<std::cmp::Ordering> {\n        Some(self.cmp(other))\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Ord for HitWithScore {\n    fn cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> std::cmp::Ordering {\n        // Sort by score descending, then by primary key ascending for tie-breaking\n        match self.score.partial_cmp(&other.score) {\n            Some(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal) | None => {\n                // On equal scores (or NaN), fall back to primary key\n                // Reversed for descending order\n                other.primary_key.cmp(&self.primary_key)\n            }\n            Some(ord) => ord.reverse(),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Result merger: combines responses from multiple shards.\npub trait Merger: Send + Sync {\n    /// Merge search results from multiple shards.\n    ///\n    /// Takes the raw JSON responses from each shard and produces\n    /// a merged result with global sorting, offset/limit applied,\n    /// and facet aggregation.\n    fn merge(\n        &self,\n        shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n        offset: usize,\n        limit: usize,\n        client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult>;\n}\n\n/// Response from a single shard.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ShardResponse {\n    /// Shard identifier.\n    pub shard_id: u32,\n\n    /// Raw JSON response from the node.\n    pub body: Value,\n\n    /// Whether this shard succeeded.\n    pub success: bool,\n}\n\n/// Merged search result (legacy, use MergedSearchResult instead).\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MergedResult {\n    /// Merged hits (globally sorted, offset/limit applied).\n    pub hits: Vec<Value>,\n\n    /// Aggregated facets.\n    pub facets: Value,\n\n    /// Estimated total hits (sum of shard totals).\n    pub total_hits: u64,\n\n    /// Processing time in milliseconds.\n    pub processing_time_ms: u64,\n\n    /// Whether the response is degraded (some shards failed).\n    pub degraded: bool,\n}\n\n/// Default implementation of Merger.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\npub struct MergerImpl;\n\nimpl Merger for MergerImpl {\n    fn merge(\n        &self,\n        shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n        offset: usize,\n        limit: usize,\n        client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult> {\n        // Convert ShardResponse to ShardHitPage\n        let shard_hits: Vec<ShardHitPage> = shard_responses\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(|sr| ShardHitPage {\n                body: sr.body,\n                success: sr.success,\n            })\n            .collect();\n\n        // Call the new merge function\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits,\n            offset,\n            limit,\n            client_requested_score,\n            facets: None,\n        };\n\n        let result = merge(input);\n\n        Ok(MergedResult {\n            hits: result.hits,\n            facets: result.facets,\n            total_hits: result.estimated_total_hits,\n            processing_time_ms: result.processing_time_ms,\n            degraded: result.degraded,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/// Merge facet distributions from all shards.\n///\n/// Facets are nested objects like `{\"color\": {\"red\": 10, \"blue\": 5}}`.\n/// We sum counts for each facet value across all shards.\n///\n/// Uses BTreeMap for stable, deterministic serialization.\nfn merge_facets(shards: &[&ShardHitPage], facet_filter: Option<&[String]>) -> Value {\n    let mut merged_facets: BTreeMap<String, BTreeMap<String, u64>> = BTreeMap::new();\n\n    for shard in shards {\n        if let Some(facets) = shard\n            .body\n            .get(\"facetDistribution\")\n            .and_then(|f| f.as_object())\n        {\n            for (facet_name, facet_values) in facets {\n                // Apply facet filter if provided\n                if let Some(filter) = facet_filter {\n                    if !filter.contains(&facet_name) {\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if let Some(values_obj) = facet_values.as_object() {\n                    let entry = merged_facets.entry(facet_name.clone()).or_default();\n\n                    for (value, count) in values_obj {\n                        let count_val = count.as_u64().unwrap_or(0);\n                        *entry.entry(value.clone()).or_insert(0) += count_val;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Convert back to JSON structure (BTreeMap ensures stable key order)\n    let result: serde_json::Map<String, Value> = merged_facets\n        .into_iter()\n        .map(|(facet_name, values)| {\n            let values_obj: serde_json::Map<String, Value> = values\n                .into_iter()\n                .map(|(k, v)| (k, Value::Number(v.into())))\n                .collect();\n            (facet_name, Value::Object(values_obj))\n        })\n        .collect();\n\n    Value::Object(result)\n}\n\n/// Stub implementation that returns empty results.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\npub struct StubMerger;\n\nimpl Merger for StubMerger {\n    fn merge(\n        &self,\n        _shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n        _offset: usize,\n        _limit: usize,\n        _client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult> {\n        Ok(MergedResult {\n            hits: Vec::new(),\n            facets: serde_json::json!({}),\n            total_hits: 0,\n            processing_time_ms: 0,\n            degraded: false,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    fn create_hit(score: f64, id: &str) -> Value {\n assert!(result.facets.get(\"size\").is_none());\n    }\n}","originalFile":"//! Result merger: combines shard results into a single response.\n\nuse crate::Result;\nuse serde_json::Value;\nuse std::collections::{BTreeMap, BinaryHeap};\n\n/// Input to the merge function.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MergeInput {\n    /// One page of hits per node in the covering set.\n    pub shard_hits: Vec<ShardHitPage>,\n\n    /// Offset to apply after merge.\n    pub offset: usize,\n\n    /// Limit to apply after merge.\n    pub limit: usize,\n\n    /// Whether the client requested the ranking score in the response.\n    pub client_requested_score: bool,\n\n    /// Facet names to include (if None, include all).\n    pub facets: Option<Vec<String>>,\n}\n\n/// A page of hits from a single shard.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ShardHitPage {\n    /// Raw JSON response from the node.\n    pub body: Value,\n\n    /// Whether this shard succeeded.\n    pub success: bool,\n}\n\n/// Merged search result.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MergedSearchResult {\n    /// Merged hits (globally sorted, offset/limit applied).\n    pub hits: Vec<Value>,\n\n    /// Aggregated facets.\n    pub facets: Value,\n\n    /// Estimated total hits (sum of shard totals).\n    pub estimated_total_hits: u64,\n\n    /// Processing time in milliseconds.\n    pub processing_time_ms: u64,\n\n    /// Whether the response is degraded (some shards failed).\n    pub degraded: bool,\n}\n\n/// Merge search results from multiple shards.\n///\n/// This is the primary entry point for result merging. It:\n/// 1. Collects all hits with scores from all shards\n/// 2. Sorts globally by `_rankingScore` descending\n/// 3. Applies offset + limit after merge\n/// 4. Strips `_rankingScore` if client didn't request it\n/// 5. Always strips `_miroir_*` reserved fields\n/// 6. Sums facet counts across shards\n/// 7. Sums `estimatedTotalHits` across shards\n/// 8. Takes max `processingTimeMs` across shards\n///\n/// Uses a binary min-heap to avoid keeping all hits in RAM when fan-out is large.\n/// Uses BTreeMap for stable facet serialization (deterministic JSON output).\npub fn merge(input: MergeInput) -> MergedSearchResult {\n    // Filter to only successful responses\n    let successful_shards: Vec<_> = input\n        .shard_hits\n        .iter()\n        .filter(|s| s.success)\n        .collect();\n\n    // Check if any shards failed (degraded mode)\n    let degraded = successful_shards.len() < input.shard_hits.len();\n\n    // Collect all hits with their ranking scores and primary keys\n    let mut all_hits: Vec<HitWithScore> = Vec::new();\n\n    for shard in &successful_shards {\n        if let Some(hits) = shard.body.get(\"hits\").and_then(|h| h.as_array()) {\n            for hit in hits {\n                let score = hit\n                    .get(\"_rankingScore\")\n                    .and_then(|s| s.as_f64())\n                    .unwrap_or(0.0);\n\n                let primary_key = hit\n                    .get(\"id\")\n                    .and_then(|id| id.as_str())\n                    .unwrap_or(\"\")\n                    .to_string();\n\n                all_hits.push(HitWithScore {\n                    score,\n                    primary_key,\n                    hit: hit.clone(),\n                });\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Use a min-heap of size offset + limit to avoid keeping all hits in RAM\n    let heap_size = input.offset + input.limit;\n    let top_hits = if all_hits.len() > heap_size * 2 {\n        // Only use heap optimization if we have significantly more hits than needed\n        // We use Reverse to turn BinaryHeap (max-heap) into a min-heap\n        use std::cmp::Reverse;\n        let mut heap: BinaryHeap<Reverse<HitWithScore>> = BinaryHeap::new();\n\n        for hit in all_hits {\n            if heap.len() < heap_size {\n                heap.push(Reverse(hit));\n            } else {\n                // Peek at the smallest (worst) hit in our top-k\n                if let Some(Reverse(worst)) = heap.peek() {\n                    // If current hit is better than our worst, replace it\n                    if hit > *worst {\n                        heap.pop();\n                        heap.push(Reverse(hit));\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Convert to sorted vector (descending by score)\n        let mut result: Vec<_> = heap.into_iter().map(|r| r.0).collect();\n        result.sort_by(|a, b| b.cmp(a));\n        result\n    } else {\n        // For smaller result sets, just sort directly\n        all_hits.sort_by(|a, b| b.cmp(a));\n        all_hits\n    };\n\n    // Apply offset and limit\n    let page: Vec<Value> = top_hits\n        .into_iter()\n        .skip(input.offset)\n        .take(input.limit)\n        .map(|mut hit_with_score| {\n            let hit = &mut hit_with_score.hit;\n\n            // Strip all _miroir_* fields (always removed)\n            if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\n                obj.retain(|k, _| !k.starts_with(\"_miroir_\"));\n            }\n\n            // Strip _rankingScore if client didn't request it\n            if !input.client_requested_score {\n                if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\n                    obj.remove(\"_rankingScore\");\n                }\n            }\n\n            hit.clone()\n        })\n        .collect();\n\n    // Aggregate facets across all shards\n    let facets = merge_facets(&successful_shards, input.facets.as_deref());\n\n    // Sum estimated total hits\n    let estimated_total_hits: u64 = successful_shards\n        .iter()\n        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\"estimatedTotalHits\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\n        .sum();\n\n    // Max processing time across all shards\n    let processing_time_ms: u64 = successful_shards\n        .iter()\n        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\"processingTimeMs\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\n        .max()\n        .unwrap_or(0);\n\n    MergedSearchResult {\n        hits: page,\n        facets,\n        estimated_total_hits,\n        processing_time_ms,\n        degraded,\n    }\n}\n\n/// A hit with its ranking score for sorting.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\nstruct HitWithScore {\n    score: f64,\n    primary_key: String,\n    hit: Value,\n}\n\nimpl PartialEq for HitWithScore {\n    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {\n        self.score == other.score && self.primary_key == other.primary_key\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Eq for HitWithScore {}\n\nimpl PartialOrd for HitWithScore {\n    fn partial_cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Option<std::cmp::Ordering> {\n        Some(self.cmp(other))\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Ord for HitWithScore {\n    fn cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> std::cmp::Ordering {\n        // Sort by score descending, then by primary key ascending for tie-breaking\n        match self.score.partial_cmp(&other.score) {\n            Some(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal) | None => {\n                // On equal scores (or NaN), fall back to primary key\n                // Reversed for descending order\n                other.primary_key.cmp(&self.primary_key)\n            }\n            Some(ord) => ord.reverse(),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Result merger: combines responses from multiple shards.\npub trait Merger: Send + Sync {\n    /// Merge search results from multiple shards.\n    ///\n    /// Takes the raw JSON responses from each shard and produces\n    /// a merged result with global sorting, offset/limit applied,\n    /// and facet aggregation.\n    fn merge(\n        &self,\n        shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n        offset: usize,\n        limit: usize,\n        client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult>;\n}\n\n/// Response from a single shard.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ShardResponse {\n    /// Shard identifier.\n    pub shard_id: u32,\n\n    /// Raw JSON response from the node.\n    pub body: Value,\n\n    /// Whether this shard succeeded.\n    pub success: bool,\n}\n\n/// Merged search result (legacy, use MergedSearchResult instead).\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MergedResult {\n    /// Merged hits (globally sorted, offset/limit applied).\n    pub hits: Vec<Value>,\n\n    /// Aggregated facets.\n    pub facets: Value,\n\n    /// Estimated total hits (sum of shard totals).\n    pub total_hits: u64,\n\n    /// Processing time in milliseconds.\n    pub processing_time_ms: u64,\n\n    /// Whether the response is degraded (some shards failed).\n    pub degraded: bool,\n}\n\n/// Default implementation of Merger.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\npub struct MergerImpl;\n\nimpl Merger for MergerImpl {\n    fn merge(\n        &self,\n        shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n        offset: usize,\n        limit: usize,\n        client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult> {\n        // Convert ShardResponse to ShardHitPage\n        let shard_hits: Vec<ShardHitPage> = shard_responses\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(|sr| ShardHitPage {\n                body: sr.body,\n                success: sr.success,\n            })\n            .collect();\n\n        // Call the new merge function\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits,\n            offset,\n            limit,\n            client_requested_score,\n            facets: None,\n        };\n\n        let result = merge(input);\n\n        Ok(MergedResult {\n            hits: result.hits,\n            facets: result.facets,\n            total_hits: result.estimated_total_hits,\n            processing_time_ms: result.processing_time_ms,\n            degraded: result.degraded,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/// Merge facet distributions from all shards.\n///\n/// Facets are nested objects like `{\"color\": {\"red\": 10, \"blue\": 5}}`.\n/// We sum counts for each facet value across all shards.\n///\n/// Uses BTreeMap for stable, deterministic serialization.\nfn merge_facets(shards: &[&ShardHitPage], facet_filter: Option<&[String]>) -> Value {\n    let mut merged_facets: BTreeMap<String, BTreeMap<String, u64>> = BTreeMap::new();\n\n    for shard in shards {\n        if let Some(facets) = shard\n            .body\n            .get(\"facetDistribution\")\n            .and_then(|f| f.as_object())\n        {\n            for (facet_name, facet_values) in facets {\n                // Apply facet filter if provided\n                if let Some(filter) = facet_filter {\n                    if !filter.contains(&facet_name) {\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if let Some(values_obj) = facet_values.as_object() {\n                    let entry = merged_facets.entry(facet_name.clone()).or_default();\n\n                    for (value, count) in values_obj {\n                        let count_val = count.as_u64().unwrap_or(0);\n                        *entry.entry(value.clone()).or_insert(0) += count_val;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Convert back to JSON structure (BTreeMap ensures stable key order)\n    let result: serde_json::Map<String, Value> = merged_facets\n        .into_iter()\n        .map(|(facet_name, values)| {\n            let values_obj: serde_json::Map<String, Value> = values\n                .into_iter()\n                .map(|(k, v)| (k, Value::Number(v.into())))\n                .collect();\n            (facet_name, Value::Object(values_obj))\n        })\n        .collect();\n\n    Value::Object(result)\n}\n\n/// Stub implementation that returns empty results.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\npub struct StubMerger;\n\nimpl Merger for StubMerger {\n    fn merge(\n        &self,\n        _shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n        _offset: usize,\n        _limit: usize,\n        _client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult> {\n        Ok(MergedResult {\n            hits: Vec::new(),\n            facets: serde_json::json!({}),\n            total_hits: 0,\n            processing_time_ms: 0,\n            degraded: false,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    fn create_hit(score: f64, id: &str) -> Value {\n        serde_json::json!({\n            \"id\": id,\n            \"_rankingScore\": score,\n            \"_miroir_shard\": 0,\n        })\n    }\n\n    fn create_shard_response(shard_id: u32, hits: Vec<Value>, total: u64) -> ShardResponse {\n        ShardResponse {\n            shard_id,\n            body: serde_json::json!({\n                \"hits\": hits,\n                \"estimatedTotalHits\": total,\n                \"processingTimeMs\": 10,\n                \"facetDistribution\": {},\n            }),\n            success: true,\n        }\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_global_sort_by_ranking_score() {\n        let merger = MergerImpl;\n\n        let hits1 = vec![\n
